	Item 1.
</U>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-VARIANT: NORMAL; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: NORMAL">
	&#160;&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-VARIANT: NORMAL; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: NORMAL">
<U>

</U>

<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">

<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	a)&#160; General Development of Business
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Educational Development Corporation (&#8220;EDC&#8221;) is the exclusive United States trade publisher of the line of educational children&#8217;s books produced in the United Kingdom by Usborne Publishing Limited (&#8220;Usborne&#8221;).&#160; We were incorporated on August 23, 1965, in the State of Delaware. Our fiscal years end on February 29(28).
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">

</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Our company motto is &#8220;The future of our world depends on the education of our children.&#160; EDC delivers educational excellence one book at a time.&#160; We provide economic opportunity while fostering strong family values.&#160; We touch the lives of children for a lifetime.&#8221;
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	As the sole United States trade publisher of the Usborne line of books, we offer over 2,000 different titles.&#160; Many are interactive in nature, including our Touchy-Feely board books, activity and flashcards, adventure and search books, art books, sticker books and foreign language books.&#160; The majority of the titles published by Kane Miller Book Publishers originally were published in other countries in their native languages.
</DIV>

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	We have a broad line of &#8216;internet-linked&#8217; books which allow readers to expand their educational experience by referring them to relevant non-Usborne websites.&#160; Our books include science and math titles, as well as chapter books and novels.&#160; We continually introduce new titles across all lines of our products.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	UBAM markets the books through commissioned consultants using a combination of direct sales, home parties, book fairs and the internet.&#160; The division had approximately 19,600 consultants in 50 states at February 29, 2016.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	EDC Publishing markets through commissioned trade representatives who call on book, toy, and specialty stores along with other retail outlets.&#160; We also do in-house marketing by telephone to these customers and potential customers.&#160; This division markets to approximately 5,000 book, toy and specialty stores.&#160; Significant orders, totaling 22% of the Publishing division&#8217;s net sales, have been received from major book chains.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Management Summary
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Educational Development Corporation is the sole distributor in the United States of the Usborne line of children&#8217;s books and is the owner of Kane Miller Book Publishers.&#160; We operate two separate divisions, EDC Publishing and Usborne Books &amp; More (&#8220;UBAM&#8221;), to sell these books.&#160; Our corporate headquarters, including the distribution facility for both divisions, is located in Tulsa, Oklahoma.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	These two divisions each have their own customer base.&#160; EDC Publishing markets its products on a wholesale basis to various retail accounts.&#160; UBAM markets its products to individual consumers as well as to school and public libraries through direct-selling consultants.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Publishing Division
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	EDC Publishing operates in a market that is highly competitive, with a large number of companies engaged in the selling of books.&#160; The Publishing division&#8217;s customer base includes national book chains, regional and local bookstores, toy and gift stores, school supply stores and museums.&#160; To reach these markets, the Publishing division utilizes a combination of commissioned sales representatives located throughout the country and a commissioned inside sales group located in our headquarters.&#160; The Vice President of the Publishing division manages sales to the national chain customers.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV>
<TABLE ID="DC084EDA3F984B1E947F617B49ABF106" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; WIDTH: 75%" CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" ALIGN="CENTER" BORDER="0">
<TR>
<TD STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-VARIANT: NORMAL; VERTICAL-ALIGN: TOP; FONT-WEIGHT: NORMAL; FONT-STYLE: NORMAL; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 47%" VALIGN="BOTTOM" COLSPAN="8">
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: CENTER; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<U>
	Publishing Division Net Revenues by Market Type

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	EDC Publishing uses a variety of methods to attract potential new customers and maintain current customers.&#160; Company personnel attend many of the national trade shows held by the book selling industry each year, allowing us to make contact with potential buyers who may be unfamiliar with our books.&#160; We actively target the national chains through joint promotional efforts and institutional advertising in trade publications.&#160; The Publishing division also participates with certain customers in a cooperative advertising allowance program, under which we pay back up to 2% of the net sales to that customer.&#160; Our products are then featured in promotions, such as catalogs, offered by the vendor.&#160; We may also acquire, for a fee, an end cap position in a bookstore (our products are placed on the end of a shelf), which in the publishing industry is considered an advantageous location in the bookstore.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	EDC Publishing&#8217;s in-house telesales group targets the smaller independent book and gift store market.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Our semi-annual, full-color, 160-page catalogs, are mailed to over 5,000 customers and potential customers.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	We also offer two display racks to assist stores in displaying our products.

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	UBAM is a multi-level direct selling organization that markets its products through independent sales representatives (&#8220;consultants&#8221;) located throughout the United States.&#160; The customer base of UBAM consists of individual purchasers, as well as school and public libraries.&#160; Revenues are generated through internet sales, home shows, book fairs and contracts with school and public libraries.&#160; This past fiscal year continued a significant shift toward online home shows via social media outlets, such as Facebook.

	An important factor in the continued growth of the UBAM division is the addition of new sales consultants and the retention of existing consultants.&#160; Current active consultants (defined as those with sales during the past six months) recruit new sales consultants.&#160; UBAM makes it easy to recruit by providing signing kits for which new consultants can earn partial or full reimbursement based on established sales criteria. &#160;UBAM provides an extensive handbook that is a valuable tool in explaining the various programs to the new recruit.

<TR>

	&#183;
</DIV>
</TD>
<TD STYLE="VERTICAL-ALIGN: TOP; WIDTH: AUTO">
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Directors
</DIV>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Upon signing up, each individual is considered a consultant.&#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Consultants receive commissions from each sale they make; the commission rate
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	is determined by the marketing program under which the sale is made.&#160; In addition, consultants receive a monthly sales bonus once their sales reach an established monthly goal.&#160; Consultants who recruit other consultants and meet certain established criteria are eligible to become team leaders.&#160; Upon reaching this level, they receive monthly override payments based upon the sales of their downline groups.
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Once team leaders reach certain established criteria, they become senior team leaders and are eligible to earn promotion bonuses on their downline groups.&#160; Once senior team leaders reach certain established criteria, they become executive team leaders, senior executive team leaders or directors.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Executive team leaders and higher may receive an additional monthly override payment based upon the sales of their downline groups.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	During fiscal year 2016, a significant shift, which began during the prior fiscal year, continued in our home party sales model from our traditional, in-person home parties.&#160; With the increased use of social media, online venues such as Facebook, have become a popular outlet for these events.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	This allows customers to &#8216;attend&#8217; online from any location.&#160; While we had marked growth in both home party net revenues, after commissions, and in internet net revenues, after commissions, this shift is most evident in the proportion of internet and home show orders to the total net revenues, after commissions.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">

<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	The increase in net revenues, after commissions, is greatly attributed to a 151% increase in the number of active consultants
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	at the end of fiscal year 2016.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	The increase in internet net revenues, after commissions, is attributed to 512% more orders placed during the period, along with a 15% increase in average order size.&#160; Customers order via the consultants&#8217; UBAM-hosted web sites, which have been customized to their own preferences.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Orders are processed through a shopping cart and the consultant receives sales credit and commission on the sales.&#160; Much of the increase in internet sales resulted from the use of social media to host virtual parties, frequently referred to as &#8220;Facebook Parties&#8221; and from the increase in the number of sales consultants.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	The school and library marketing program increase is attributed to a 53% increase in the number of orders, offset by the average order size decreased of 2% over the prior fiscal year.&#160;
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;
</FONT>
	Much of this change is a result of the increase in the number of sales consultants.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	School and library sales are made by consultants who have received additional, specialized training which allows them to sell to schools and libraries.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	The UBAM consultant is the only source that a library or school has for most of our titles.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	They are not available through school supply distribution companies.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	This program includes book fairs which are held with an organization as the sponsor.
</FONT>
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 5.03PT">
	&#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	The consultant provides promotional materials to acquaint parents with the books.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Parents turn in their orders at a designated time.&#160; The book fair program generates free books for the sponsoring organization.&#160; UBAM also has a
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Reach for the Stars
</FONT>
	fundraiser program.&#160; This is a pledge-based reading incentive program that provides cash and books to the sponsoring organization and books for the children.
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	The increase in home party sales, including the discontinued category of &#8220;direct sales&#8221;, after commissions, is attributed to a 227% increase in the total number of orders, offset by a 56% decrease in average order size.&#160; Much of this change is a result of the increase in the number of sales consultants.&#160; Consultants contact individuals (&#8220;hostesses&#8221;) to hold book shows in their homes.&#160; The consultant assists the hostess in setting up the details for the show and makes a presentation at the show and takes orders for the books.&#160; The hostess earns free books based upon the total sales at the show, including online orders. These online orders are reported as internet sales, which has resulted in smaller average home show order sizes.&#160; Customer specials are available for customers when they order a selected amount.&#160; Additionally, home shows provide an excellent opportunity for recruiting new consultants.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Our fund-raising program,
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Cards for a Cause
</FONT>
	, increased 135% in sales, after commissions, over the prior year.&#160; This resulted from a 30% increase in the number of orders and a 71% increase in the average size of these orders over the prior fiscal year.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Organizations sell variety boxes of greeting-type cards and keep a portion of the proceeds to help support themselves and their related causes.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Transportation revenues increased 270% during fiscal year 2016. &#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Transportation revenues are based on sales order size, with minimums per order depending on order type. &#160;This increase is partially due to the increase in the number of smaller orders for which a standard minimum is applied, along with a full year benefit of a 20% increase in that minimum which occurred halfway through fiscal year 2015.
</FONT>
</DIV>

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Our Board of Directors adopted a stock repurchase plan in which we may purchase up to an additional 500,000 shares as market conditions warrant.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	When management believes the stock is undervalued and when stock becomes available at an attractive price, we can utilize free cash flow to repurchase shares.&#160; Management believes this enhances the value to the remaining shareholders and that these repurchases will have no adverse effect on our short-term and long-term liquidity.
</DIV>

<A NAME="FIS_UNIDENTIFIED_TABLE_12"></A>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Fiscal Year 2016 Compared with Fiscal Year 2015
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	The following presents an overview of our results of operations for years ended February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015.&#160; We had earnings before income taxes of $3,545,900 for fiscal year 2016 compared with $1,402,500 for fiscal year 2015.
</DIV>

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	UBAM&#8217;s gross sales increased 138.0% or $33,274,800 during fiscal year 2016 to $57,385,300 when compared with fiscal year 2015.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	This increase is attributable to a 151% increase in the number of independent sales consultants, with resulting increases in all types of sales, including internet, school and library/book fair, home parties, and fund raisers. &#160;The overall number of orders was up 398% due to increases in internet, home show, school and library, and fund raiser orders.&#160; Average sales per order for this division were down 48%, primarily due to a shift from larger home party orders to multiple individual online orders per internet-based party.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	EDC Publishing&#8217;s gross sales decreased 5.4% or $1,300,800 during fiscal year 2016 when compared with fiscal year 2015.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Sales increased by 5.0% to smaller retail stores and decreased by 14.4% to national chain stores.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	UBAM&#8217;s discounts and allowances were $9,927,900 in fiscal year 2016 and $4,533,600 in fiscal year 2015.&#160; Most sales by UBAM are at retail.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	As a part of UBAM&#8217;s marketing programs, discounts between 40% and 50% of retail are offered on selected items at various times throughout the year.&#160; The discounts and allowances in the UBAM division will vary from year to year depending upon the marketing programs in place during any given year
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; COLOR: #0000FF">
	.&#160;
</FONT>
	UBAM&#8217;s discounts and allowances were 17.3% of UBAM&#8217;s gross sales in fiscal year 2016 and 18.8% in fiscal year 2015.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	EDC Publishing&#8217;s discounts and allowances are a much larger percentage of gross sales than discounts and allowances in the UBAM division due to the different customer markets that each division targets.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	The Publishing division&#8217;s discounts and allowances were $12,133,600 in fiscal year 2016 and $12,739,500 in fiscal year 2015.&#160; To be competitive with other wholesale book distributors, EDC Publishing sells at discounts between 48% and 55% of the retail price, based upon the quantity of books ordered and the dollar amount of the order.&#160; EDC Publishing&#8217;s discounts and allowances were 52.9% of their gross sales in fiscal year 2016 and 52.6% in fiscal year 2015.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Transportation revenues increased $3,884,400 or 263.2% in fiscal year 2016, due primarily to the increase in UBAM gross sales during the year and the shift in sales to more, smaller internet-based orders, which each are subject to a flat minimum shipping charge.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Also, we realized the benefit of a full year with a 20% increase in the minimum shipping charge made during fiscal year 2015.
</DIV>

<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Cost of sales increased 60.6% in fiscal year 2016 when compared with fiscal year 2015.&#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Our cost of products is 22% to 28% of the gross sales price, depending upon the product.&#160; The percentage change in gross sales to the percentage change in cost of sales, depends largely on the mix of products sold.&#160; Approximately 67% of our products come from one vendor, where the cost of the products is a fixed percentage of the retail price.&#160; Cost of sales is the inventory cost of product sold (including the cost of the product itself and inbound freight charges), along with royalties accrued for sales of Kane Miller titles for which we have royalty payment contracts.&#160; The costs of our distribution network are not included in our cost of sales, but rather in our operating and selling expenses.
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Operating and selling expenses include purchasing and receiving, inspection, warehousing, and other costs of our distribution network.&#160; These costs totaled $2,865,700 in fiscal year 2016 and $1,259,500 in fiscal year 2015.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	In addition to costs associated with our distribution network (noted above), operating and selling costs include expenses of the Publishing and UBAM divisions, along with the order entry and customer service functions
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; COLOR: #0000FF">
	.&#160;
</FONT>
	Operating and selling expenses as a percentage of gross sales were 24.2% for fiscal year 2016 and 19.7% for fiscal year 2015.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Sales commissions for EDC Publishing increased $800 for the fiscal year ended 2016. &#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Sales commissions for this division fluctuate depending upon the amount of sales made to our &#8220;house accounts,&#8221; which are our largest customers and do not have any commission expense associated with them, and sales made by our outside sales representatives.&#160; Publishing division sales commissions are paid on net sales and were 3.2% for fiscal year 2016 and 3.0% for fiscal year 2015.
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Sales commissions for UBAM increased $11,219,300.&#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	UBAM division sales commissions are paid based on the retail price of non-promotional products sold and were 30.9% of UBAM gross sales for fiscal year 2016 and 26.9% for fiscal year 2015. &#160;The fluctuation in the percentages of commission expense to gross sales is the result of the type of sale.&#160; Internet sales, home shows, book fairs, school and library sales and fundraiser sales have different commission rates.&#160; Also, another factor contributing to the fluctuations in the percentages is the payment of overrides and bonuses, both dependent on consultants&#8217; monthly sales and downline sales.&#160; The increase in sales commissions is the result of higher gross sales in the UBAM division.
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	General and administrative expenses include the executive department, accounting department, information services department, general office management and building facilities management.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	General and administrative expenses as a percentage of gross sales were 2.9% for fiscal year 2016 and 4.2% for fiscal year 2015.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	The tax provision for fiscal year 2016 was $1,426,600.&#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	The effective rate for fiscal year 2016 was 40.2% and for fiscal year 2015 was 38.7%.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Our effective tax rate is higher than the Federal statutory rate due to an IRS audit settlement for $67,800 of our 2012 tax year, state income and franchise taxes.
</FONT>
</DIV>

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Contractual Obligations
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	We are a smaller reporting company and are not required to provide this information.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Critical Accounting Policies
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Our discussion and analysis of our financial condition and results of operations are based upon our financial statements, which have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States.&#160; The preparation of these financial statements requires us to make estimates and judgments that affect the reported amounts of assets, liabilities, revenues and expenses, and related disclosures of contingent assets and liabilities.&#160; On an on-going basis, we evaluate our estimates, including those related to our valuation of inventory, allowance for uncollectible accounts receivable, allowance for sales returns, long-lived assets and deferred income taxes.&#160; We base our estimates on historical experience and on various other assumptions that are believed to be reasonable under the circumstances, the results of which form the basis for making judgments about the carrying values of assets and liabilities that are not readily apparent from other sources.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Actual results may materially differ from these estimates under different assumptions or conditions.&#160; Historically, however, actual results have not differed materially from those determined using required estimates. &#160;Our significant accounting policies are described in the notes accompanying the financial statements included elsewhere in this report.&#160; However, we consider the following accounting policies to be more significantly dependent on the use of estimates and assumptions.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Stock-Based Compensation
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	We account for stock-based compensation whereby share-based payment transactions with employees, such as stock options and restricted stock, are measured at estimated fair value at date of grant and recognized as compensation expense.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Revenue Recognition
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
	Sales are recognized and recorded when products are shipped.&#160; Products are shipped FOB shipping point.&#160; UBAM&#8217;s sales are paid at the time the product is ordered.&#160; These sales accounted for 83% and 65% of net revenues in fiscal years 2016 and 2015, respectively.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
	Estimated allowances for sales returns are recorded as sales are recognized and recorded.&#160; Management uses a moving average calculation to estimate the allowance for sales returns.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160; &#160;
</FONT>
	We are not responsible for product damaged in transit.&#160; Damaged returns are primarily from the retail stores.&#160; The damages occur in the stores, not in shipping to the stores.&#160; It is industry practice to accept returns from wholesale customers.&#160; Transportation revenue represents the amount billed to the customer for shipping the product and is recorded when the product is shipped.&#160; Management has estimated and included a reserve for sales returns of $100,000 for the years ended February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Allowance for Doubtful Accounts
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	We maintain an allowance for estimated losses resulting from the inability of our customers to make required payments.&#160; An estimate of uncollectible amounts is made by management based upon historical bad debts, current customer receivable balances, age of customer receivable balances, customers&#8217; financial conditions and current economic trends.&#160; Management has estimated an allowance for doubtful accounts of $401,900 and $234,500 as of February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015, respectively.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Inventory
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Management continually estimates and calculates the amount of noncurrent inventory.&#160; The inventory arises due to occasional purchases of book inventory in quantities in excess of what will be sold within the normal operating cycle due to minimum order requirements of our primary supplier.&#160; Noncurrent inventory was estimated by management using the current year turnover ratio by title.&#160; All inventory in excess of 2 &#189; years of anticipated sales was classified as noncurrent inventory.&#160; Noncurrent inventory balances prior to valuation allowances were $469,000 and $718,900 at February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015, respectively.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Inventories are presented net of a valuation allowance.&#160; Management has estimated and included a valuation allowance for both current and noncurrent inventory.&#160; This allowance is based on management&#8217;s identification of slow moving inventory on hand.&#160; Management has estimated a valuation allowance for both current and noncurrent inventory of $325,000 and $393,100 as of February 29, 2016 and 2015, respectively.
</DIV>
<DIV ID="DSPFPAGEBREAKAREA" STYLE="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10PT; CLEAR: BOTH; MARGIN-TOP: 10PT">
<DIV ID="DSPFPAGEFOOTER">
</DIV>
<DIV ID="DSPFPAGENUMBERAREA" STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: CENTER">
<FONT ID="DSPFPAGENUMBER" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 8PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: NORMAL; FONT-STYLE: NORMAL">
	13
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV ID="DSPFPAGEBREAK" STYLE="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: ALWAYS">
<HR STYLE="BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0PX; HEIGHT: 2PX; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0PX; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0PX; COLOR: #000000; CLEAR: BOTH; MARGIN: 4PX 0PX; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0PX; WIDTH: 100%; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #000000" NOSHADE="NOSHADE">
</DIV>
<A NAME="eolPage14"></A>
<DIV ID="DSPFPAGEHEADER" STYLE="WIDTH: 100%">
<A HREF="#EDC10K022916_HTM_TABLEOFCONTENTS">
	Table of Contents
</A>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Our product line contains approximately 2,000 titles, each with different rates of sale, depending upon the nature and popularity of the title.&#160; Almost all of our product line is saleable as the books are not topical in nature and remain current in content today as well as in the future.&#160; Most of our products are printed in Europe, China, Singapore, India, Malaysia and Dubai resulting in a three to four-month lead-time to have a title reprinted and delivered to us.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Our principal supplier, based in England, generally requires a minimum reorder of 6,500 or more of a title in order to get a solo print run.&#160; Smaller orders would require a shared print run with the supplier&#8217;s other customers, which can result in more lengthy delays to receive the ordered title.&#160; Anticipating customer preferences and purchasing habits requires historical analysis of similar titles in the same series.&#160; We then place the initial order or re-order based upon this analysis.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	These factors and historical analysis have led Management to determine that 2 &#189; years represents a reasonable estimate of the normal operating cycle for our products.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	New Accounting Pronouncements
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	The Financial Accounting Standards Board (&#8220;FASB&#8221;) periodically issues new accounting standards in a continuing effort to improve standards of financial accounting and reporting.&#160; We have reviewed the recently issued pronouncements and concluded that the following recently issued accounting standards apply to us.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	In May 2014, FASB issued ASU No. 2014-09, and amended with ASU No. 2015-14 &#8220;Revenue from Contracts with Customers,&#8221; which provides a single revenue recognition model which is intended to improve comparability over a range of industries, companies and geographical boundaries and will also result in enhanced disclosures.&#160; The changes are effective for fiscal years, and interim periods within those years, beginning after December 15, 2017, which means the first quarter of our fiscal year 2019.&#160; We are currently reviewing the ASU and assessing the potential impact on our financial statements.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	In August 2015, FASB issued ASU No. 2015-15 &#8220;Interest&#8212;Imputation of Interest,&#8221; which modifies the presentation and subsequent measurement of debt issuance costs associated with line-of-credit arrangements.&#160; These changes allow an entity to defer and present debt issuance costs as an asset and subsequently amortize the deferred debt issuance costs ratably over the term of the line-of-credit arrangement, regardless of whether there are any outstanding borrowings on the line-of-credit arrangement.&#160; The changes are effective for financial statements issued for annual periods beginning after December 15, 2015, and interim periods within those annual periods, which means the first quarter of our fiscal year 2017.We are currently reviewing the ASU and assessing the potential impact on our financial statements.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	In November 2015, FASB issued ASU No. 2015-17, which is intended to improve how deferred taxes are classified on organizations&#8217; balance sheets by eliminating the current requirement for organizations to present deferred tax liabilities and assets as current and noncurrent in a classified balance sheet.&#160; Instead, organizations will now be required to classify all deferred tax assets and liabilities as noncurrent.&#160; The changes are effective for financial statements issued for annual periods beginning after December 15, 2016, and interim periods within those annual periods, which means the first quarter of our fiscal year 2018.&#160; We anticipate this ASU having minimal impact on our financial statements.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	In February 2016, FASB issued ASU No. 2016-02, &#8220;Leases,&#8221; which is intended to establish a comprehensive new lease accounting model.&#160; The new standard clarifies the definition of a lease, requires a dual approach to lease classification similar to current lease classifications, and causes lessees to recognize leases on the balance sheet as a lease liability with a corresponding right-of-use asset.&#160; The new standard is effective for interim and annual periods beginning after December 15, 2018, which means the first quarter of our fiscal year 2020.&#160; The new standard requires a modified retrospective transition for capital or operating leases existing at or entered into after the beginning of the earliest comparative period presented in the financial statements.&#160; We are currently reviewing the ASU and evaluating the potential impact on our financial statements.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	In March 2016, FASB issued ASU No. 2016-09, &#8220;Compensation - Stock Compensation: Improvements to Employee Share-Based Payment Accounting,&#8221; which is intended to simplify several aspects of the accounting for share-based payment transactions, including the income tax consequences, classification of awards as either equity or liabilities, and classification on the statement of cash flows.&#160; The new standard is effective for interim and annual periods beginning after December 15, 2016, which means the first quarter of our fiscal year 2018.&#160; We are currently reviewing the ASU and evaluating the potential impact on our financial statements.
</DIV>

<DIV STYLE="FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">

	Item 9A.
</U>
</FONT>
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 5.5PT">
	&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
<U>
	CONTROLS AND PROCEDURES
</U>
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	An evaluation was performed of the effectiveness of the design and operation of our disclosure controls and procedures pursuant to Exchange Act Rule 13a-15(e) and 15d-15(e) as of February 29, 2016. &#160;This evaluation was conducted under the supervision and with the participation of our management, including our Chief Executive Officer and our Controller/Corporate Secretary (Principal Financial and Accounting Officer).
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Based on that evaluation, these officers concluded that our disclosure controls and procedures were effective to ensure that information required to be disclosed in reports that we file or submit under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 is accumulated and communicated to them, as appropriate, to allow timely decisions regarding required disclosure and is recorded, processed, summarized and reported in accordance within the time periods specified in Securities and Exchange Commission rules and forms.&#160; It should be noted that the design of any system of controls is based in part upon certain assumptions about the likelihood of future events.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	During the fourth fiscal quarter of the fiscal year covered by this report on Form 10-K, there have been no changes in our internal control over financial reporting that have materially affected or are reasonably likely to materially affect, our internal control over financial reporting.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	&#160;
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN'; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: CENTER; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	MANAGEMENT&#8217;S REPORT ON INTERNAL CONTROL OVER FINANCIAL REPORTING
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	Our management is responsible for establishing and maintaining adequate internal control over financial reporting, as such term is defined in Rule 13a-15(f) of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;).&#160; Under the supervision and with the participation of our management, including our President and our Controller, we evaluated the effectiveness of our internal control over financial reporting based on the framework in INTERNAL CONTROL-INTEGRATED FRAMEWORK issued by the Committee of Sponsoring Organizations of the Treadway Commission in 1992. &#160;All internal control systems, no matter how well designed, have inherent limitations. &#160;Therefore, even those systems determined to be effective can provide only reasonable assurance with respect to financial statement preparation and presentation. &#160;Projections of any evaluation of effectiveness to future periods are subject to the risk that controls may become inadequate because of changes in conditions, or that the degree of compliance with the policies or procedures may deteriorate.&#160; Based on our evaluation under that framework and applicable SEC rules, our management concluded that our internal control over financial reporting was effective as of February 29, 2016. &#160;The original framework was updated with the issuance of the 2013 Internal Control &#8211; Integrated Framework by the Committee of Sponsoring Organizations of the Treadway Commission. Our management has not yet implemented the 2013 Framework, but does not deem it impacting our effective assessment conclusion.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 36PT">
	This annual report does not include an attestation report of our registered public accounting firm regarding internal control over financial reporting. &#160;Management&#8217;s report was not subject to attestation by our registered public accounting firm pursuant to rules of the Securities and Exchange Commission that permit us to provide only management&#8217;s report in this annual report.

<EFX_AUDITORS_OPINION>
<A NAME="FIS_AUDITORS_OPINION"></A>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: CENTER; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	REPORT OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	To the Board of Directors and Shareholders
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 12PT">
	Educational Development Corporation
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 12PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 12PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	We have audited the accompanying balance sheets of
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; COLOR: #000000">
	Educational Development Corporation as of February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015,
</FONT>
	and the related statements of earnings, shareholders&#8217; equity and cash flows for the years then ended.&#160; These financial statements are the responsibility of the Company&#8217;s management.&#160; Our responsibility is to express an opinion on these financial statements based on our audits.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	We conducted our audits in accordance with the standards of the Public Company Accounting Oversight Board (United States).&#160; Those standards require that we plan and perform the audit to obtain reasonable assurance about whether the financial statements are free of material misstatement.&#160; The Company is not required to have, nor were we engaged to perform, an audit of its internal control over financial reporting.&#160; Our audits included consideration of internal control over financial reporting as a basis for designing audit procedures that are appropriate in the circumstances, but not for the purpose of expressing an opinion on the effectiveness of the Company&#8217;s internal control over financial reporting.&#160; Accordingly, we express no such opinion.&#160; An audit also includes examining, on a test basis, evidence supporting the amounts and disclosures in the financial statements, assessing the accounting principles used and significant estimates made by management, as well as evaluating the overall financial statement presentation.&#160; We believe that our audits provide a reasonable basis for our opinion.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	In our opinion, the financial statements referred to above present fairly, in all material respects, the financial position of
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; COLOR: #000000">
	Educational Development Corporation
</FONT>
	as of
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; COLOR: #000000">
	February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015,
</FONT>
	and the results of its operations and its cash flows for the years then ended, in conformity with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	/s/ HOGANTAYLOR LLP
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	Tulsa, Oklahoma
</DIV>

</DIV>

<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">

</DIV>
<DIV>
<TABLE ID="EA5AF055DD8743A08AFB1EF91874B719" CLASS="DSPFLISTTABLE" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; WIDTH: 100%" CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0">
<TR>
<TD STYLE="VERTICAL-ALIGN: TOP; WIDTH: 30PX; ALIGN: RIGHT">
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	1.
</DIV>
</TD>
<TD STYLE="VERTICAL-ALIGN: TOP; WIDTH: AUTO">
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
	SUMMARY OF SIGNIFICANT ACCOUNTING POLICIES
</DIV>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 10.25PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 10.25PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Nature of Business
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
	Educational Development Corporation (&#8220;we&#8221;, &#8220;our&#8221;, &#8220;us&#8221;, or &#8220;the Company&#8221;) distributes books and publications through our EDC Publishing and Usborne Books &amp; More (&#8220;UBAM&#8221;) divisions to book, toy and gift stores, libraries and home educators located throughout the United States (&#8220;U.S.&#8221;).&#160; We are the sole U.S. distributor of books and related items, which are published by an England-based publishing company, Usborne, our primary supplier.&#160; We are also in the direct publishing market through our ownership of Kane Miller Book Publishers.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Estimates
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
	Our financial statements were prepared in conformity with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America, which requires management to make estimates and assumptions that affect the amounts and disclosures in the financial statements.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Actual results could differ from these estimates.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Business Concentration
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
	A significant portion of our inventory purchases are concentrated with Usborne.&#160; Purchases from them were approximately $20.0 million and $12.2 million for the years ended February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015, respectively.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Total inventory purchases for those same periods were approximately $29.8 million and $15.3 million, respectively.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Cash and Cash Equivalents
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
	Cash and cash equivalents are maintained at financial institutions and, at times, balances may exceed federally insured limits. &#160;We have never experienced any losses related to these balances.&#160; Insurance coverage on our cash balances was limited to $250,000 and our cash balances exceed federally insured limits. &#160;The majority of payments due from banks for third party credit card transactions process within two business days.&#160; These amounts due are classified as cash and cash equivalents.&#160; Cash and cash equivalents also include demand and time deposits, money market funds and other marketable securities with maturities of three months or less when acquired.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Accounts Receivable
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
	Accounts receivable are uncollateralized customer obligations due under normal trade terms generally requiring payment within thirty days from the invoice date.&#160; Extended, seasonal dating is frequently available for orders of minimum quantities or amounts.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Trade accounts are stated at the amount management expects to collect from outstanding balances.&#160; Delinquency fees are not assessed.&#160; Payments of accounts receivable are allocated to the specific invoices identified on the customers&#8217; remittance advice.&#160; Accounts receivable are carried at original invoice amount less an estimated reserve made for returns and discounts based on quarterly review of historical rates of returns and expected discounts to be taken.&#160; The carrying amount of accounts receivable is reduced, if needed, by a valuation allowance that reflects management&#8217;s best estimate of the amounts that will not be collected.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
	&#160;
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
	&#160;Management periodically reviews accounts receivable balances and, based on an assessment of historical bad debts, current customer receivable balances, age of customer receivable balances, customers&#8217; financial conditions and current economic trends, estimates the portion of the balance that will not be collected.&#160; Management provides for probable uncollectible amounts through a charge to earnings and a credit to a valuation account based on its assessment of the current status of the individual accounts.&#160; Balances which remain outstanding after management has used reasonable collection efforts are written off through a charge to the valuation allowance and a credit to trade accounts receivable.&#160; Recoveries of trade receivables previously written off are recorded as income when received.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Inventories
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Inventories are stated at the lower of cost or market.&#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Cost is determined using the first-in-first-out method.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	We present a portion of our inventory as a noncurrent asset.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Occasionally we purchase book inventory in quantities in excess of what will be sold within the normal operating cycle due to minimum order requirements of our primary supplier.&#160; These excess quantities are included in noncurrent inventory.&#160; We estimate noncurrent inventory using the current year turnover ratio by title.&#160; All inventory in excess of 2&#189; years of anticipated sales is classified as noncurrent inventory.
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Inventories are presented net of a valuation allowance.&#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Management has estimated and included an allowance for slow moving inventory for both current and noncurrent inventory.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	This allowance is based on management&#8217;s analysis of inventory on hand at February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015.
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV ID="DSPFPAGEBREAKAREA" STYLE="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10PT; CLEAR: BOTH; MARGIN-TOP: 10PT">
<DIV ID="DSPFPAGEFOOTER">
</DIV>

<FONT ID="DSPFPAGENUMBER" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 8PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: NORMAL; FONT-STYLE: NORMAL">

</FONT>

<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
	Property, plant and equipment are stated at cost and depreciated on a straight-line basis over the estimated useful lives, as follows:

<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.3PT">
	Capitalized projects that are not placed in service are recorded as in progress and are not depreciated until the related assets are placed in service.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Income Taxes
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
	We account for income taxes using the liability method.&#160; Under this method, deferred tax assets and liabilities are determined based on the difference between the financial statement and the tax basis of assets and liabilities using the current tax laws and rates.&#160; A valuation allowance is established when necessary to reduce deferred tax assets to the amounts that are &#8220;more likely than not&#8221; to be realized.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Revenue Recognition
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Sales are recognized and recorded when products are shipped.&#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Products are shipped FOB shipping point.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	The UBAM division&#8217;s sales are paid at the time the product is ordered.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	These sales accounted for 83% of net revenues in fiscal year 2016 and 65% in fiscal year 2015.&#160; Sales which have been paid but not shipped are classified as deferred revenue on the balance sheet.
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
	Allowances for estimated sales returns are recorded as sales are recognized and recorded.&#160; Management uses a moving average calculation to estimate the allowance for sales returns.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	We are not responsible for product damaged in transit. &#160;Damaged returns are primarily from the retail stores related to damages which occur in the stores, not in shipping to the stores.&#160; It is industry practice to accept returns from wholesale customers.&#160; Management has estimated and included a reserve for sales returns of $100,000 as of February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
	Transportation revenue represents the amount billed to the customer for shipping the product and is recorded when the product is shipped.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Advertising Costs
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Advertising costs are expensed as incurred. &#160;
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Advertising expenses, included in selling and operating expenses in the statements of earnings, were $531,500 and $367,300 for the years ended February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015, respectively.
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Shipping and Handling Costs
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
	We classify shipping and handling costs as operating and selling expenses in the statements of earnings.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Shipping and handling costs were $8,655,600 and $3,719,300 for the years ended February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015, respectively.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
	&#160;
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<STRONG>
<EM>
	Interest Expense
</EM>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
</STRONG>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF">
	Interest related to our outstanding debt is recognized as incurred.&#160; Interest expense, classified separately in the statements of earnings, were $244,900 and $54,000 for the years ended February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015, respectively.
</FONT>
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
<BR STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; TEXT-ALIGN: LEFT; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5PT">
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Earnings per Share
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
	Basic earnings per share (&#8220;EPS&#8221;) is computed by dividing net earnings by the weighted average number of common shares outstanding during the period.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	Diluted EPS is based on the combined weighted average number of common shares outstanding and dilutive potential common shares issuable which include, where appropriate, the assumed exercise of options.&#160; In computing Diluted EPS, we have utilized the treasury stock method.
</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4PT">

<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD; FONT-STYLE: ITALIC">
	Long-Lived Asset Impairment
</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 10PT; FONT-FAMILY: 'TIMES NEW ROMAN', TIMES, SERIF; FONT-WEIGHT: BOLD">
	&#8212;
</FONT>
	We review the value of long&#8209;lived assets for impairment whenever events or changes in circumstances indicate that the carrying amount of an asset may not be recoverable based on estimated future cash flows.
<FONT ID="TRGRRTFTOHTMLTAB" STYLE="FONT-SIZE: 6PT">
	&#160;&#160;
</FONT>
	No impairment was noted as a result of such review during the years ended February 29, 2016 and February 28, 2015.
